This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using `Agda` `v2.5.3`.

## Requirements

`Agda` has a pragma to be compatible with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="562" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="574" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="586" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Equality type  also called Identity type can be defined as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="684" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="690" class="Number">4</a> <a id="692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#701" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a>
<a id="696" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_≡_"></a><a id="701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#701" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="705" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#706" class="Bound">a</a><a id="707" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="709" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#710" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="712" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="714" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#706" class="Bound">a</a><a id="719" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="721" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#722" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="724" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#710" class="Bound">A</a><a id="727" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="729" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#710" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="733" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="735" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#706" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="741" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise }
  Given functions $f : A \rightarrow B$ and $g : B \to C$, define
  their composite $g\circ f:A\to C$.
  Show that we have $h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$.

We define the composition operation in `Agda` as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2019" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2023" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2025" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2027" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2028" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2030" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2032" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2033" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2035" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2036" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2040" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2028" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2045" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2047" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2051" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2030" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2056" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2058" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2058" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2062" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2032" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2067" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Exercise 1.2

{: .exercise }
  Derive the recursion principle for products $\rec_{A\times B}$
  using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
  are valid. Do the same for $\Sigma$-types.

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    {:.eq}
      $$ \rec_{ A \times B}
        : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
      $$

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $ \rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$\proj_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$ and $\proj_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$,
then $\rec_2$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\rec_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\proj_1 c,~\proj_2 c).
\end{align*}
$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{ A \times B}$ and $\rec_1$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $\proj_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$ and
$\proj_2 :  \prod {(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\proj_1 p)$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \U}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\rec_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\proj_1 c)~(\proj_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$ and $\rec_2$.
</div>

Now, I'm gonna use the universe levels from Agda in
the following exercises, including this one:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4206" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4211" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="4218" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a>
  <a id="4235" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="4241" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4242" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4247" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4249" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a><a id="4252" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4254" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#611" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="4259" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4261" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="4265" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Σ-type (sigma type) definition (see the definition without projections
[here](https://github.com/jonaprieto/hott-book/blob/master/other/prelim.agda#L20)):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4448" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁"></a><a id="4455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4455" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="4462" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="4471" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ"></a><a id="4478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Record">Σ</a> <a     <a id="4538" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_"></a><a id="4550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="4558" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁"></a><a id="4570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4570" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="4576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4487" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₂"></a><a id="4586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4586" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="4592" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4499" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="4596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4570" class="Field">proj₁</a>

  <a id="4605" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="4612" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="4619" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$
that we provide.

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5242" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₁"></a><a id="5249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5249" class="Module">×-Def₁</a> <a id="5256" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $A\times B$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\proj_{1}(x) , \proj_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6385" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="6452" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>

Projections and $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6839" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Fun₂"></a><a id="6846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6846" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a> <a id="6853" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6854" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="6856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6856" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6857" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6859" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6861" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6863" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6854" class="Bound">i</a><a id="6868" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6870" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6874" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6856" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6879" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6881" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="6889" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6894" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6509" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="6901" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="6907" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6530" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="6912" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="6913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6586" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="6916" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6609" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="6923" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6690" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="6930" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="6935" class="Comment">-- propositional uniqueness principle:</a>

  <a id="7384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7296" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#749" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#749" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7400" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#749" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \U}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$
</p>

        <a id="7845" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7847" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="7849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7849" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7851" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7705" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7854" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7856" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7858" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7716" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7861" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7863" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7865" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7818" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="7867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7849" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6586" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7856" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7873" class="Symbol">))</a>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$\Sigma$-types, i.e. show induction and verify that the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

Projections and uniqueness propositional principle:

  <a id="9244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9093" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9250" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9252" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9252" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9254" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9256" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9258" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#749" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\U} C \to (C \to C) \to \N \to C $
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $\rec$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $\N$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10143" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def"></a><a id="10150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10150" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10156" class="Keyword">where</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10663" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="10670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10670" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="10676" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="10684" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10150" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10695" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10701" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10170" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="10703" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10188" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="10709" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10201" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="10714" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10718" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10222" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="10729" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10735" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10249" class="Function">rec</a><a id="10739" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="10744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10744" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10750" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10752" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10753" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10755" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10757" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="10760" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10762" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10753" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10766" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10753" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10771" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10753" class="Bound">C</a><a id="10774" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10776" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10778" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10170" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="10780" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10753" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="10786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10744" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10790" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10792" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10795" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10188" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="10806" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10792" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="10813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10744" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10817" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10819" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10201" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="10830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10831" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10833" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10839" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10744" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10817" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10819" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10851" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10852" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10996" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>

           <a id="11249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11122" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11250" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11440" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="11447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="11453" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="11496" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10222" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11507" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10249" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11517" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11521" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10373" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a> <a id="11532" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10400" class="Function">ind</a><a id="11542" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11546" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10670" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11557" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10744" class="Function">ite</a><a id="11567" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11569" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11056" class="Function">rec₂</a><a id="11573" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11578" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6509" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11590" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6530" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11600" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6609" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11607" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6690" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11614" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6586" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11619" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="11638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11638" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="11644" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11646" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11647" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11649" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11651" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11654" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11656" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11659" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11647" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11662" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11664" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11667" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10170" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11671" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11647" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11675" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11647" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11678" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="11688" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11690" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11692" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link ### Exercise 1.5

{: .exercise}

  Show that if we define $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \two)} \rec_{\two} (\U, A , B, x),$$
  then we can give a definition of $\ind_{A + B}$ for which the
  definitional equalities holds.

To solve this problem, let me introduce the $\two$ type, which is, the
type only two constructors, the **Booleans**.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12556" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="12563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12563" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="12570" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12579" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="12584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="12586" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12588" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12592" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="12602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="12604" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="12612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="12614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12664" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="12671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="12678" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12687" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12563" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a>  <a id="12700" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="12708" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="12709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="12710" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="12711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="12712" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13429" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="13472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13472" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13474" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13476" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13477" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13472" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13482" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13644" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="13651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13651" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="13658" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13667" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13116" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="13679" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13236" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="13689" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="13691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13371" class="Function">inl</a><a id="13694" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13429" class="Function">inr</a><a id="13698" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="13702" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13706" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12563" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13718" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13726" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13728" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13730" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Rec₁.rec"></a><a id="13735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13735" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13741" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13743" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13744" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13746" class="Bound">j</a><a id="13747" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13750" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13752" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13756" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13744" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13761" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13763" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13764" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13766" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13768" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13746" class="Bound">j</a><a id="13773" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="13781" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13783" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13750" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13786" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13764" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13789" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13752" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13764" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13805" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13750" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13236" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="13819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13752" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13821" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13823" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13764" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="13827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13735" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13831" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13833" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13840" class="Bound">a</a><a id="13841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13843" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13831" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13840" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="13851" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13735" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13855" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13855" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13857" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13859" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13864" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13864" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13865" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13867" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13857" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13864" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png){: width="%50" }

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14261" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Ind₁"></a><a id="14268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14268" class="Module">+-Ind₁</a> <a id="14275" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14284" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14289" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13116" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14296" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13236" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14306" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13371" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14311" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13429" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14315" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14320" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14324" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12563" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14336" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14344" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14346" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14348" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Ind₁.ind"></a><a id="14353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14353" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="14357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14359" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14361" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14362" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14364" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14364" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14365" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14367" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14370" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14372" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14374" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14362" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14379" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14381" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13236" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14370" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14392" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14394" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14398" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14364" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14399" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="14407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14409" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14411" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14411" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="14413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14368" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14416" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13371" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="14427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14411" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14428" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14437" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14439" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14441" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14443" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14370" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14446" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14448" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13429" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="14457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14441" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14458" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14467" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14470" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14474" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13236" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14370" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14479" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14470" class="Bound">p</a>

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\rec_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\U\, A\, B\, x)$,
then we can give a definition of $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15244" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₃"></a><a id="15251" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15251" class="Module">×-Def₃</a> <a id="15258" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15266" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12563" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="15278" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15284" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12602" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="15286" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12612" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="15288" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15289" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12584" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="15290" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15292" class="Keyword">public</a>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $\rec{\N}$.
Verify that $(\N,+,0,\times,1)$ is a semiring using only
$\ind{\N}$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

}}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17337" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17339" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10170" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17342" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17344" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17346" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10170" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17347" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17349" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17352" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17354" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10201" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="17360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10188" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="17364" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17366" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17369" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17371" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17373" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17375" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17212" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="17383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17373" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17371" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17373" class="Bound">m</a><a id="17389" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$.

2. Additive commutativity: $\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $\mathsf{Fin} : \N \to \U$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\N} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $A$, we have $\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="19281" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="19288" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19288" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="19295" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19303" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19308" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="19315" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="19332" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="19337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19337" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19343" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19345" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19347" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19348" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19348" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19349" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19351" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19352" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19353" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="19363" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19348" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19367" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19369" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19371" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19373" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19352" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19377" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="19379" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19352" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="19385" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19337" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19391" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19392" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19393" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19398" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="19404" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="19418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19419" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="19437" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19438" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="19459" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19460" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19470" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19477" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19478" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19480" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19392" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19483" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19486" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19489" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19491" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19492" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19495" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="19515" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19516" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="19540" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19541" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="19566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19567" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19574" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19575" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19577" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19392" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19581" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19583" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19585" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19587" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19591" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19594" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19597" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19600" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="19621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19622" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19630" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19633" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19636" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19644" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19392" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19650" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19652" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19654" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19656" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19659" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19395" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19662" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
$\prod\limits_{i,j : \N}\ (i + j = j + i).$
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20015" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20022" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20029" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20037" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10150" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20050" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10373" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20063" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17106" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="20074" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="20080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17147" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="20084" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $p : x \equiv y$, then the function
$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png){: width="%30" }

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it suffices to show a function
$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$ such that we can prove
$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$ and
$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$.

Let's define the function $g$.
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\trans~(\sym~p)~m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>

($(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$):
Let be $m : x ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~p~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~(\trans~p~(\sym~p))~m\\
                        &= \trans~\refl_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>
($ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$):
Let be $n : y ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= (\trans~(\sym~p)~(\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= \trans~(\trans~(\sym~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \trans~\refl_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $A : \U$
and families $B : A  \to U$ and $C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \U$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $f$ and $g$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
defined by $f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$ and $g(z,c) :\equiv (\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.f-g"></a><a id="23620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23620" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23626" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23628" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23629" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23633" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23636" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23638" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23639" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23629" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23645" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23647" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23650" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23652" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23653" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23629" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23639" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23663" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23665" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23668" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23678" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23681" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23629" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23639" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23693" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23653" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23696" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="23706" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23319" class="Function">f</a> <a id="23710" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23711" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="23713" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23629" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23716" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23718" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="23720" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23639" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23723" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23725" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="23727" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23653" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23460" class="Function">g</a> <a id="23735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23681" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23736" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#701" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="23740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23681" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="23744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23620" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23748" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23750" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#749" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.g-f"></a><a id="23760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23760" class="Function">g-f</a> <a id="23764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23766" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23768" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23769" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23771" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23773" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23776" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23778" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23779" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23769" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23787" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23790" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23792" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23793" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4478" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23769" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23779" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23803" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23805" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23808" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23818" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23820" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23821" ### Exercise 2.13

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.13">
Show that $(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>

The following text is from [Jdoughertyii](https://github.com/jdoughertyii/hott-exercises/blob/master/Ch02.v).<br/>
The result essentially says that $\two$ is equivalent to itself in two ways:
the identity provides one equivalence, and negation gives the other.  So we
first define these.  $\id_{\two}$ is its own quasi-inverse; we have
$\id_{\two} \circ \id_{\two} \equiv \id_{\two}$, so $\id_{\two}
\circ \id_{\two}
\sim \id_{\two}$ easily.  $\lnot$ is also its own quasi-inverse, since for
any $x$, $\lnot\lnot x = x$.
To show the result, we need to map $\id_{\two}$ and $\lnot$ onto $\two$ is
a quasi-invertible way.  But we need to define this map on all of $\two \simeq \two$.
So for any $h : \two\simeq \two$, let $f(h) = h(\zero_{\two})$, and define
$g : \two \to (\two \simeq \two)$ by

{: .equation}
  $$ g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_{\two}$$ and  $$g(\one_{\two}) = \lnot.$$

To show that these are quasi-inverses,
note first that whatever else is the case, an equivalence
$\two \simeq \two$ can't be a constant function, which we can prove by a case
analysis. Each of $f(\zero_{\two})$ and $f(\one_{\two})$ is in $\two$, so it is
either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.

So we have the cases:
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = f(\one_{\two})$, in which case we can apply $f^{-1}$ to either side to get a contradiction, or
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = \lnot f(\one_{\two})$. In which case we have the result
Showing that $f \circ g \sim \id_{\two}$ is easy, since we can do it by
cases.  We have

$$\begin{align*}
  f(g(\zero_{\two})) &= f(\id_{\two}) = \id_{\two}(\zero_{\two}) = \zero_{\two}
  \\
  f(g(\one_{\two})) &= f(\lnot) = \lnot \zero_{\two} = \one_{\two}
\end{align*}$$

For the other direction, suppose that $h : \two \simeq \two$ and that
function extensionality holds.
$h(\zero_{\two})$ is either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.  If the first, then
because $h$ isn't constant we have $h(\one_{\two}) = \lnot h(\zero_{\two}) =
\one_{\two}$, hence $h = \id_{\two}$.  Furthermore,

$$g(f(h)) = g(h(\zero_{\two})) = g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_\two = h$$

The same argument works for the other case. So $f$ is an equivalence, and
$(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.

</div>

### Exercise 2.14

{: .exercise}

  Suppose we add to type theory [the equality reflection
  rule](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IlfQjWqrK6I) which says that if there is
  an element $p : \id(x,y) $, then in fact $ x :\equiv y$. Prove that
  for any $p : \id(x,x)$ we have $p \equiv \refl_x$.

  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14.png){: width="25%" }


{: .proof}
  Proof.<br/>
  We first fix the type of $$\refl_x$$ in order to apply effectively
  path induction.<br/>
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14b.png){: width="100%" }
  Now, $$\refl_x$$ and $$p : x = y$$ in the formulation of path induction
  are well-typed. Therefore, by path induction, we show that
  $$\id(p,\mathsf{refl_{x}})$$. Let be $$x : A$$ and $$C :\equiv
  \prod_{y : A} \prod_{p : x \equiv y }\ p \equiv \refl_{x}$$.
  It sufficies to show and inhabitant of $$C(x, \refl_{x})$$, and this is
  $$\refl_{\refl_x} : \refl_x = \refl_x$$.
  By the equation reflection rule, since we have an inhabitant of $$p \equiv
  \refl_x$$, we conclude these terms are judgemental equal, i.e., $$p \equiv \refl_x$$.

### Exercise 2.17

<div class="exercise">
<ul>
  <li> Show that if $A \simeq A$  and $B \simeq B'$, then $(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$. </li>
  <li> Give two proofs of this fact, one using univalence and one not using it, and show that the two proofs are equal.</li>
  <li> Formulate and prove analogous results for the other type formers: $\Sigma$, $\to$, $\Pi$, and $+$. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
  Proof.<br/>
  - Assuming Univalence.
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.17.png){: width="50%" }
  - Without Univalence, it is easy to prove
  that the function $h$ defined as follows gives us the
  equivalence that we are looking for.
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h : (A\times B) \to (A'\times B')\\
  &h (a , b) = (f\, a, g\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  With the inverse:
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h^{-1} : (A'\times B') \to (A\times B)\\
  &h^{-1} (a , b) = (f^{-1}\, a, g^{-1}\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  To prove these proofs are equal it is suffices to
  show these underlying functions are equal.
</div>

## Chapter 3

To solve the following exercises, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $A$ is a **set** if for all $x, y : A$ and
all $p, q : x \equiv y$, we have $ p \equiv q$. In a proposition
we have

$$\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).$$

- The type for equivalence from $A$ to $B$

$$ (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f), $$
where
$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \id_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \id_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$ be two sections of a
type family $P : A \to \U$. A **homotopy** from $f$ to $g$
is a dependent function of type

$$(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).$$

### Exercise 3.1

{: .exercise"}
  Prove that if $A\simeq B$ and $A$ is a set, then so is $B$.


<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1" markdown="1" >
Proof.<br/>
Let be $x,y : B$ and $p : x \equiv_{B} y$ and $q : x \equiv_{B} y$.
We need to prove $ p \equiv q$.<br/>
Since $A\simeq B$ then there is a function $f : A \to B$ and some
$g : B \to A$ such that $f \circ g \sim id_{B}$.
Using this function $g$ over the path $p$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.

We do the same but this time over the path $q$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $A$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $m$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us

$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$


By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=(\text{transporting by using} f \sim g)\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} q\\
  &=p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$

Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.2

{: .exercise}
  Prove that if $A$ and $B$ are sets, then so is $A+B$.

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12.

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2" markdown="1">
Proof.<br/>

Let be $x, y : A + B$, and paths $p : x \equiv y$, $q : x \equiv
y$. Let's get a path $p \equiv q$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$ and $y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$, for
some $a, b : A$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $A$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

By path algebra we have $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$p$ and $q$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $p\equiv q$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.4

{: .exercise }
  Show that $A$ is a mere proposition if and only
  if $A\to A$ is contractible.

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Proof. <br/>
- We must to show an inhabitant of the following type:

$$
\mathsf{isProp}(A) \to \sum\limits_{f : A \to A}\, \prod\limits_{g : A \to A } f = g.
$$

This is my proposed term:

$$
t :\equiv λ \mathsf{Aprop} \to (\id_{A}, λ (g : A \to A) \to \mathsf{funext} (\lambda (x : A) \to \mathsf{Aprop}~(\mathsf{id}~x)~(g~x)).
$$

- If $A → A$ is contractible, all functions in this type are equal,
then in particular given $x, y : A$, the constant functions $f(w) \equiv x$
and $g(w) \equiv y$ are equal. Then, $\mathsf{happly} (f =_{A \to A} g, w) : x = y$.
Therefore $$A$$ is a mere proposition.

</div>
